Partner 13: CENTRE FOR RENEWABLE ENERGY SOURCES & SAVING, PIC: 999646014 
Short Name CRES Country Greece 
 
Type RTO Website www.cres.gr 
Brief description of the organisation 
CRES is a public entity supervised by the Ministry of Environment and Energy, and has financial and 
administrative independence. CRES is active in the fields of Renewable Energy Sources (RES), Rational 
Use of Energy (RUE) and Energy Saving (ES). Its primar y aim is to promote technological applications in 
the above-mentioned fields both at a national and international level. CRES was appointed by Law 2244/94 
and Law 2702/99 as the National Centre for Coordination in the fields of its activity. It acts as an advisor to 
the Greek State, and has established a highly visible profile of a strong and reliable national energy centre.  
CRES has a scientific staff of more than 120 highly qualified engineers and other scientists (among total 
personnel of 160) and, over  the years, has participated in more than 600 European and national projects. 
These include R&D projects, demonstration projects, development of energy information systems & models, 
assessment and analysis of energy policies, feasibility studies, technical  and economic studies, market 
research, as well as training and promotional activities on the RES/RUE/ES related issues.  
CRES co-operates with other institutes, organizations, universities, consultants, international organizations 
(such as the IEA, UNESCO, ISES, PLEA, IEC, CEN, etc), while it is an active member of various European 
and international networks, such as the EnR, MEDENER, EUFORES, OPET, EUREC Agency, etc.  
CRES has supported numerous municipalities and regional authorities to develop sustainable energy plans, 
energy efficiency interventions and promotional campaigns and has also developed national energy 
sustainable energy schemes for municipalities. Since F ebruary 2012 CRES is the Greek National 
Coordinator for the Covenant of Mayors. Additionally, CRES has strong competencies on borehole heat 
exchangers and heat pumps technology research, demonstration and market development. Specific expertise 
and skills include technology optimization, operation, monitoring and evaluation, technical & financial case 
studies compilation, sectorial analysis, innovation system analysis, business models, development of market 
introduction supporting measures, as well as in management and dissemination actions.  
The Department of Buildings in the Division of Energy Efficiency in CRES has long experience on: 
• Technical support of the state on the energy performance of buildings and ES, of the industry on the 
optimisation of buil ding materials and elements and of the private sector (including households, offices, 
hospitals, industrial, educational and tourist buildings) with the bioclimatic design of buildings and open 
spaces, the optimisation of energy performance of the building  and the use of RES and ES applications in 
buildings. 
• Conduction of energy audits in buildings and industrial plants.  
• Development of passive solar systems and new ES technologies on the building envelope. 
• Support of the public and private sector on ES investments with new financial mechanisms. 
• Contribution on the design of ES at national level and the implementation of EU directives, 
regarding energy savings in the building sector. 
The laboratory facilities of the Buildings dept. provide with accredited testing services for the determination 
of the thermal characteristics of building materials and components. It can also carry out measurements for 
the evaluation of the efficiency of boilers, photovoltaic and solar thermal systems. Additionally, it i s 
equipped with all the necessary measuring devices to carry out energy audits of various building types (i.e. 
residential, office, industrial plants, hospitals, hotels) and various other laboratory equipment and software 
tools for the determination of dif ferent aspects which affect the energy conservation and efficiency in 
buildings. 
Role in the project 
CRES will collaborate in the general coordination activities in WP1. CRES will collaborate to obtain the 
heating and cooling needs for the Greek end-user (MAND) in WP2. CRE  will analyze the measurements   
and study the possible scenarios to optimise the operation of the prototype solar thermal system  in WP7. 
Finally, CRES will carry out dissemination activities to interested parties.

Brief description of the organisation 
IRIS Technology Group is an advanced engineering Group that was established in Barcelona in 2007. Since 
2011, it also operates from Dublin (Ireland) whereas the Barcelona office is referred to as IRIS Technology 
Solutions S.L. It specialises in the manufac ture and integration of Process Analytical Technology (PAT) -
based real -time quality monitoring solutions for the process industries and IoT systems for smart 
manufacturing, predominantly targeted at the food, pharmaceutical and chemical industries. In part icular, 
our product line comprises proprietary state -of-the-art IR analysers for at -line and in -line process 
monitoring.  
On the one hand, our solutions are based on the latest developments in photonics in the fields of MEMs, 
Near Infrared Spectroscopy, Hy perspectral Imaging, and Raman. On the other hand, we leverage ICTs, 
whereby we apply Machine learning, Artificial Intelligence and Data Mining techniques for predictive and 
active control, as well as for decision support systems. In addition to photonics -based analysers, we also 
work with IoT sensors for enabling equipment and machinery for smart manufacturing and transitioning 
industry to the Industry4.0 paradigm. Our solutions are cloud -based for mobility, remote monitoring and 
multi-site applications.  
Our Innovation Division which is governed by an Innovation Committee comprising Senior Management, 
and an Innovation Unit for managing and executing the companies innovation roadmap, has 3 core strategic 
lines, for shaping the Factory of the Future: 
• New optical photonics-based technologies and PAT systems for production process optimisation 
• ICTs (Artificial intelligence / machine learning, IOT & cloud platforms) 
• Circular and Bio-based Economy: digitalization and waste valorisation 
In addition to running an internal R&D programme, as well as carrying our various joint private projects 
with industry partners, our Innovation Division is highly experienced in working in collaborative R&D 
projects in H2020 (both as coordinators and partners), principally in the SPIRE, FoF, and BBI programmes. 
The company was established in 2007 and currently employs 60+ staff with a turnover of € 5 M. It is 
equipped with engineering workshops (3), food testing and wet chemistry laboratory, optics labs (2), and an 
electronics/telecommunications lab. IRIS is ISO 9001:2008 certified and also is certified under UNE -EN-
ISO 166002: Management Systems R&D&i. We are also certified by the local (Catalonian) government as 
a provider of technological R&D services (Tecnio Certification). IRIS is a member of the following sectorial 
networks: SPIRE, SPIE and SECPHO, in addition to regional industrial collectives such as Smart Space 
(association of companies and organisations that specialise in the ‘smartification’ of industry).

Partner 16: UNIVERSITÀ DEGLI STUDI DELLA CAMPANIA), PIC: 999848356

Brief description of the organisation 
The University of Campania "Luigi Vanvitelli" (Second University of Naples, before the change of name), 
known as SUN, was established in 1991 (Decree MURST, 25 March) with the aim of relieving the 
overcrowded conditions of the major Neapolitan university known as the “Federico II”. On the official date 
of November 1st 1991, the Vanvitelli University began to function autonomously with nineteen thousand 
enrolments and eight faculties located in five different te rritorial areas of Caserta and Naples.  Currently, 
there are thirty thousand students attending the Vanvitelli’s 18 Departments.  The University’s multicampus 
structure has two offices for its Rector: one in Naples and the other in Caserta. Currently, ther e are thirty 
thousand students attending the UCLV’s 16 Departments. 
The Dipartimento di Ingegneria dell'Università degli Studi della Campania “Luigi Vanvitelli” is involved in 
numerous national and international research activities. Strategic areas are Aer ospace and Mechanical 
Engineering, Computer and Automatic Engineering, Electronic and Telecommunications Engineering, 
Civil, Building Structures and Environmental Engineering as well as Design and History as well as Electrical 
Engineering, Chemical and Materials Engineering. Several laboratories with advanced equipment are in the 
Department. In addition, numerous agreements, contracts and research collaboration agreements have been 
stipulated with national and international Universities, associations, consortia and companies. 
The Research Group of Heat Transfer  (HTGroup) develops a strong research activity in Heat Transfer 
and Energy and collaborates with several Regional, National and International companies and industries 
interested in Energy and Applied Heat Transfer.  
In its Laboratories are developed fundamental and applied heat transfer in: 
• Micro and nanotechnologies, thin films, nanofluids, micro and nanochannels, porous media and 
foams 
• Material and manufacturing processes by localized sources such as laser and electron beam 
A particular interest is oriented to thermo  fluid-dynamics in air -conditioning, energy saving, renewable 
energy and energy efficiency improvement in buildings, safety in historical buildings and infrastructures. 
By the experiences acquired along the years, the HTGroup has developed thermal design and optimization 
techniques in systems and components. Some particular experience s are oriented in electronic cooling 
systems, systems and components for energy conversion in renewable energy with strong experience in high 
concentration solar energy and high thermal temperature storage 
Role in the project 
The SUN team will have an active and supportive role in WP1 and WP2. SUN will support the end-users in 
the thermal design and optimization of single components and system. SUN will also participate to in WP9 
based on its experience in organization scientific conferences and participation to COST action.

Brief description of the organisation 
MANDREKAS SA is a family owned dairy. It started with Dimitrios Mandrekas the founder back in 1954. 
He produced and sold over the counter Greek traditional yogurt from sheep/cow milk. In 1984 Evangelos 
Mandrekas took over after coming back from his studies in England (B.Sc , M.Sc in Engineering). 
 
In 1991 a new plant was commissioned outside Corinth -Greece where modern yogurt production is still 
taking place. The business grew up and MANDR EKAS SA is one of the largest private label yogurt 
producers in the country. Our main core business is production of Greek Yogurt, branded and private label. 
We also have developed exports in Europe and USA where Greek Yogurt has become a household novelty. 
 
We produce all types of yogurt plus some yogurt desserts (tzatziki sauce ) and milk desserts, (rice pudding, 
custard cream and chocolate). Today, we employ 55 people and our motto is FFF (Fast, Flexible, Fresh). 
We can deliver all over the world either from our factory in Greece or from selected co -production dairies 
around the world, where the product is produced with our recipes and technology, under our supervision. 
Role in the project 
MAND will provide information about their heating and cooling needs in WP2. Mainly, MAND will offer 
its facilities for the installation of the project in WP7. MAND will provide the staffs’ technical expertise on 
the theoretical and practical aspects of the  project . MAND will help with m onitoring and assistance with 
the collection of data or other information required by the other participants . MAND will also collaborate 
with the sustainability assessment of the proposal concept in WP8. Finally, MAND will help with the impact 
activities in WP9.

in departments such as production, technical and warehouse departments. Prior to that, he was a 
Logistics Analyst for Wal-Mart Canada, completing projects aiming to  increase the efficiencies of the 
logistics network of the company.  
Since 2015, he has joined MANDREKAS S.A, taking over the position of the operations manager and 
eventually the CEO. The company has shown a steady growth through the years of the recession, 
increasing its market presence and sales within Greece and other countries across Europe, Middle East, 
US and Asia.

Engineering from Kings College, London. He is considered one of the few experts in Greek Yogurt

The Foundation for the Promotion of Industrial Innovation (F2I2) was created in 1993 by the Technical University 
of Madrid (UPM) in collaboration with the Ministry of Industry and Energy (currently the Ministry of Industry, 
Commerce and Tourism - MINCOTUR), at the request of the Higher Technical School of Industrial Engineers 
(ETSII) of the UPM. 
This Foundation supposes a new impulse in the already long tradition of work towards the  Industry that the 
Laboratories, Institutes and Departments of the ETSII have been carrying out since its creation, concretized in the 
accomplishment of works of investigation and development, essays, calibrations, consultancies, surveys or studies, 
in a l arge number of scientific and technical areas, mainly in the electrical, vehicle and thermal fields, both for 
national and international industry. 
These tasks are linked to its close relationship with MINCOTUR, in technical support work in the development of 
electrotechnical regulations, industrial product control campaigns and international technical support in EU work 
groups. 
The Foundation has an important number of professionals of recognized prestige, adequate facilities and equipment. 
It has the Offic ial Central Electrotechnical Laboratory (LCOE) and laboratories arranged with another 23 of the 
ETSII, in addition to a client-oriented administrative and management support. 
Main tasks in the project: 
Foundation F2I2 professionals will provide expertise in dealing with glasses and mirrors. They have a 
lab for breaking glasses in order to study their behavior in particular circumstances (as automobile 
crashes). They have also demonstrated capabilities to build electrical systems for different types of 
motion, from sun trackers to electric vehicles. Their work will be much more oriented to practical 
tasks in building and managing proto-industrial systems, which is the role assigned to them in this 
project. Therefore, they will collaborate with UPM in the construction of the SunDial labScale 
concentrators on sub-task 6.1.1.
